- isnull(F4,0)
- isnull(F6,0)
 from  ptj_cumulat inner join F100 on ptj_cumulat.F10003 = F100.F10003 
  where an=ent.An and Luna=ent.Luna and ptj_cumulat.F10003 = ent.F10003)

 where year(Ziua)=ent.An AND MONTH(Ziua)=ent.Luna AND Ptj_intrari.F10003=ent.F10003)

Eroarea:   The column 'Comentarii' was specified multiple times for 'A'.
-----------------------------------------------------
Data:    07.04.2020 09:00:53
Pagina:    General
Eveni:     IncarcaDT
Eroarea:   with ptj_intrari_2 as (select A.* from Ptj_Intrari A 
                                LEFT JOIN Ptj_Contracte C ON A.IdContract=C.Id
                                LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607
                                 LEFT JOIN "viewCategoriePontaj" CTG ON A.F10003 = CTG.F10003   
                                WHERE 1=1 AND '2020-04-01' <= A.Ziua AND A.Ziua <= '2020-04-30' )
                                SELECT *,
                                (SELECT ',Ziua' + CASE WHEN Y.Zi <= X.F10023 THEN CONVERT(nvarchar(10), DAY(Y.Zi)) END
                                FROM F100 X
                                INNER JOIN tblZile Y ON '2020-04-01' <= Y.Zi AND Y.Zi <= '2020-04-30'
                                WHERE X.F10003=A.F10003
                                FOR XML PATH ('')) AS ZileLucrate,
                                (SELECT ',Ziua' + CASE WHEN Y.Zi < CONVERT(date,X.F10022) OR CONVERT(date,X.F10023) < Y.Zi THEN CONVERT(nvarchar(10), DAY(Y.Zi)) END
                                FROM F100 X
                                INNER JOIN tblZile Y ON '2020-04-01' <= Y.Zi AND Y.Zi <= '2020-04-30'
                                WHERE X.F10003=A.F10003
                                FOR XML PATH ('')) AS ZileGri
                                FROM (
                                SELECT TOP 100 PERCENT COALESCE(3,1) AS IdRol, st.Denumire AS StarePontaj, isnull(zabs.Ramase, 0) as ZileCONeefectuate, isnull(zlp.Ramase, 0) as ZLPNeefectuate, A.F100901, CAST('2020-04-01' AS datetime) AS ZiuaInc, 
                                CONVERT(VARCHAR, A.F10022, 103) AS DataInceput, CONVERT(VARCHAR, ddp.DataPlecare, 103) AS DataSfarsit,  A.F10008 + ' ' + A.F10009 AS AngajatNume, C.Id AS IdContract, 
                                Y.Norma, Y.F10002, Y.F10004, Y.F10005, Y.F10006, Y.F10007,

                                INNER JOIN (SELECT F10003 , [2020-03-01] AS "Ziua1", [2020-03-02] AS "Ziua2", [2020-03-03] AS "Ziua3", [2020-03-04] AS "Ziua4", [2020-03-05] AS "Ziua5", [2020-03-06] AS "Ziua6", [2020-03-07] AS "Ziua7", [2020-03-08] AS "Ziua8", [2020-03-09] AS "Ziua9", [2020-03-10] AS "Ziua10", [2020-03-11] AS "Ziua11", [2020-03-12] AS "Ziua12", [2020-03-13] AS "Ziua13", [2020-03-14] AS "Ziua14", [2020-03-15] AS "Ziua15", [2020-03-16] AS "Ziua16", [2020-03-17] AS "Ziua17", [2020-03-18] AS "Ziua18", [2020-03-19] AS "Ziua19", [2020-03-20] AS "Ziua20", [2020-03-21] AS "Ziua21", [2020-03-22] AS "Ziua22", [2020-03-23] AS "Ziua23", [2020-03-24] AS "Ziua24", [2020-03-25] AS "Ziua25", [2020-03-26] AS "Ziua26", [2020-03-27] AS "Ziua27", [2020-03-28] AS "Ziua28", [2020-03-29] AS "Ziua29", [2020-03-30] AS "Ziua30", [2020-03-31] AS "Ziua31" FROM 
                                (SELECT F10003, ValStr, Ziua From Ptj_Intrari_2 WHERE '2020-03-01' <= CAST(Ziua AS date) AND CAST(Ziua AS date) <= '2020-03-31') AS source  
                                PIVOT  (MAX(ValStr) FOR Ziua IN (  [2020-03-01], [2020-03-02], [2020-03-03], [2020-03-04], [2020-03-05], [2020-03-06], [2020-03-07], [2020-03-08], [2020-03-09], [2020-03-10], [2020-03-11], [2020-03-12], [2020-03-13], [2020-03-14], [2020-03-15], [2020-03-16], [2020-03-17], [2020-03-18], [2020-03-19], [2020-03-20], [2020-03-21], [2020-03-22], [2020-03-23], [2020-03-24], [2020-03-25], [2020-03-26], [2020-03-27], [2020-03-28], [2020-03-29], [2020-03-30], [2020-03-31] )) pvt
                                ) pvt ON X.F10003=pvt.F10003
                                LEFT JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=X.F10003 
                                LEFT JOIN F1001 B ON A.F10003=B.F10003 
                                LEFT JOIN (SELECT R.F10003, MIN(R.Ziua) AS ZiuaMin FROM Ptj_Intrari_2 R WHERE YEAR(R.Ziua)= 2020 AND MONTH(R.Ziua)= 3 GROUP BY R.F10003) Q ON Q.F10003=A.F10003
                                LEFT JOIN Ptj_Intrari_2 Y ON A.F10003=Y.F10003 AND Y.Ziua=Q.ZiuaMin
                                LEFT JOIN Ptj_tblStariPontaj K ON K.Id = ISNULL(X.IdStare,1) 
                                LEFT JOIN Ptj_Contracte C on C.Id = Y.IdContract 
                                LEFT JOIN F089 DR ON DR.F08902 = A.F1009741 
                                 LEFT JOIN "viewCategoriePontaj" CTG ON A.F10003 = CTG.F10003 
                                OUTER APPLY dbo.DamiNorma(X.F10003, '2020-03-31') dn 
                                OUTER APPLY dbo.DamiDataPlecare(X.F10003, '2020-03-31') ddp 

							    LEFT JOIN F002 S2 ON Y.F10002 = S2.F00202
							    LEFT JOIN F003 S3 ON Y.F10004 = S3.F00304
							    LEFT JOIN F004 S4 ON Y.F10005 = S4.F00405

							    LEFT JOIN F005 H ON Y.F10006 = H.F00506
							    LEFT JOIN F006 I ON Y.F10007 = I.F00607

							    LEFT JOIN F007 S7 ON B.F100958 = S7.F00708
                                LEFT JOIN F008 S8 ON B.F100959 = S8.F00809

                                LEFT JOIN F062 L ON Y.F06204Default=L.F06204

                                LEFT JOIN F718 Fct ON A.F10071=Fct.F71802

                                WHERE X.An = 2020 AND X.Luna = 3 
                                ORDER BY AngajatNume) A
                                WHERE 1=1  AND A.F10003 IN ( SELECT X.F10003 FROM (  SELECT B.f10003 FROM relGrupAngajat B INNER JOIN Ptj_relGrupSuper C ON B.IdGrup = C.IdGrup WHERE C.IdSuper =2 AND C.IdRol=3 GROUP BY B.f10003 UNION SELECT B.f10003 FROM relGrupAngajat B INNER JOIN Ptj_relGrupSuper C ON B.IdGrup = C.IdGrup INNER JOIN F100Supervizori D ON D.F10003 = B.F10003 AND D.IdSuper = (-1 * C.IdSuper) AND (100 * 2020 + 3 BETWEEN isnull(100 * year(D.DataInceput) + MONTH(D.DataInceput), 190000) AND isnull(100 * year(D.DataSfarsit) + MONTH(D.DataSfarsit), 210000))  WHERE D.IdUser =2 AND C.IdRol=3 GROUP BY B.F10003) X  WHERE X.F10003 IN (SELECT S.F10003 FROM F100 S WHERE S.F10025 <> 900 AND CONVERT(date,S.F10022) <> CONVERT(date,S.F100993)  AND F10022 <= '2020-3-31' AND '2020-3-01' <= F100993 ) GROUP BY X.F10003)

                                                            THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
                                                            ELSE 0 
                                                            END DEBLOCARE  
                                                            FROM USERS X WHERE UPPER(F70104)='HR'
